 Using a new technique, scientists have discovered the date of formation of frozen ice sheet on the ancient lake of Antarctica
 vaigyanikon ke anusaar, purvi antarctic main barf kii yah chadar 1
 40 million years old
 yah shodh us dharna kaa samarthan karata he jiske anusaar, 30-50 lakh saal pehle pliosin (atinutan kaal) yug ke dauraan bhi barf kii yah chadar bade str par nahin pighali thi, haalanki tab carbon diaksaide kii sandratha aaj hi ke samaan thi
 Jane Willinbring, assistant professor at the University of Pennsylvania, USA, states, "the Pliocene era is sometimes compared to the notion where globans think of large natural events occurring on Earth as the warming progresses
 " wilinbring ke anusaar, "yah shodh hamaari us ummid ko bal detaa he jahaan purvi antarctic kii barf kii chadar vartmaan or bhavishya ke mausamon ke anusaar tiki rah sakati he
 "comments kuch vaigyanikon kaa maananaa he ki yah barf kii chadar pliosin yug ke dauraan kuch sthitiyon main pighali thi
 At the same time, some scientists believe that this sheet is completely about 1
 4 karod saalon se jami he
 Willinbring and his colleagues, however, hoped to clarify its history
 iske liye unhone mahadweep ke purvi hisse ke madhya sukhi ghaatiyon main sthit antarctic ke fris pahaado kii yatra kii he
 The lake has an accumulation of various substances on the surface under an ice sheet roughly equal to a foot, and is known for freshwater and various fossils
 is nai takanic kii sahaayta se vaigyanik jhilein ke un vibhinn padaartho kii aayu kaa akalan kar paae hai or vaigyanikon ke anusaar in padaartho kii aayu 1
 1 from 4 crore years
 75 karod saal ke kareeb hai
 This means, says Willinberg, that this substance is much older than at the time where people are thinking that glaciers are decreasing over Antarctica
 isse sabit hota he ki antarctic main glaciaron ke pighalane kii jo dharanaen saamne aa rahi hai vah puri tarah sahi nahin hai
 This research has been published in the journal Scientific Reports
 america kii pencylvania uniwarsity ke sahaayak professor jine wilinbring kaa kahana he, "pliosin yug kii tulana kabhi-kabhi us dharna se kii jaati he jahaan globan varmig ke lagaataar badhane par prithvi par hone vaali badi prakritik ghatnaon ke bare main sochate hai

 Gangaur festival is celebrated on Chaitra Shukla Tritiya
 ise gauri tritiya bhi kehete hai
 This festival is especially for women
 is din mahilaayein shiv-parvati kii aradhana karti hai
 It is said that on this day Lord Shiva gave Parvati ji and then Parvati ji a boon of good fortune to all women and society
 is din suhaaginen vrath rakhti hai
 Worship Maa Durga's ninth form to attain accomplishment
 
 
 kab se aarambh hoti he poojagangaur kii puja holi ke duusare din (caitra krishna pratipada) se aarambh ho jaati he
 From this day, women worship Gangaur every day and on the day of Chaitra Shukla Dwitiya (sinjare), they go to the river, pond or lake to offer water to the worshiped Gangaurs
